 /**
 * Initializes AEMs components when application is ready.
 * Application is ready after loading RequireJS.
 */
 function App() {
 	this.components = [];
 }
 
 /**
 * Adds components to be initialized when application is ready.
 * @param {Function} func a function to initialize a component
 */
 App.prototype.addComponent = function(func) {
 	this.components.push(func);
 };
 
 /**
 * Call this function when application is ready to initialize AEM components.
 */
 App.prototype.initComponents = function() {
 	for (var i = 0; i < this.components.length; i++) {
 		this.components[i]();
 	}
 };
 
 // Initialize app
 window.app = new App();

 			* Gets cookie value of intern_ip and

 			* If the cookie is not set, `NA` will be returned
 			* @returns {String}
 			*/
 			function getValue() {
 			// Get name followed by anything except a semicolon
 			var cookie = RegExp("internal_ip[^;]+").exec(document.cookie);
 			// Get everything after the equal sign, or an empty string if the cookie name not found
 			var cookieValue = ((cookie && cookie[0]) ? cookie[0].replace(/^[^=]+./,"") : "");

 				return "intern";
 			} else if (cookieValue === "false") {

 			}

 			}
